create table customers
( 
    cid varchar(50) not null,
    age varchar(50) not null,
    phone varchar(50) not null,
    email varchar(50) not null,
    street varchar(50) not null,
    city varchar(50) not null,
    state varchar(50) not null,
    zipcode varchar(50) not null,
    fname varchar(50) not null,
    lname varchar(50) not null,

    primary key (cid)
);
create table vehicle
( 
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    seating int not null,
    make varchar(50) not null,
    model varchar(50) not null,
    mpg varchar(7) not null,
    vtype varchar(5) not null,

    primary key (vin)
);

create table rent
( 
    rental_id varchar(50) not null,
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    cid varchar(50) not null,
    start_date date not null,
    end_date date not null,

    primary key (rental_id),
    foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin),
    foreign key (cid) references customers(cid)
);

create table truck
( 
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    load_capacity varchar(50) not null,

    primary key (vin),
    foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin)
);
create table suv
( 
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    cargo varchar(50) not null,

    primary key (vin),
    foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin)
);
create table car
( 
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    doors int not null,
    type varchar(50) not null,

    primary key (vin),
    foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin)
);
create table reservation
( 
    rid varchar(50) not null,
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    cid varchar(50) not null,
    ccnum varchar(16) not null,
    insurance boolean not null default 0,
    start_date date not null,
    end_date date not null,
    

    primary key (rid),
    foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin),
    foreign key (cid) references customers(cid)
);
create table service
( 
    sid varchar(50) not null,
    vin varchar(50) not null,
    descrip varchar(3000) not null,
    start_date date not null,
    end_date date not null,
    work_location varchar(3000) not null,

    primary key (sid),
    foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin)
);

ALTER TABLE reservation 
	add constraint ccmin check (char_length(ccnum) >= 13);

ALTER TABLE customers
	add constraint phonemin check (char_length(phone) >= 10);
ALTER TABLE customers
	add constraint zipmin check (char_length(zipcode) >= 4);
ALTER TABLE customers
	add constraint state_name check(state in('AK', 'AL', 'AR', 'AS', 'AZ', 'CA', 'CO', 'CT', 'DC', 'DE', 'FL', 'GA', 'GU', 'HI', 'IA', 'ID', 'IL', 	'IN', 'KS', 'KY', 'LA', 'MA', 'MD', 'ME', 'MI', 'MN', 'MO', 'MP', 'MS', 'MT', 'NC', 'ND', 'NE', 'NH', 'NJ', 'NM', 'NV', 'NY', 'OH', 'OK', 'OR', 'PA', 'PR', 'RI', 'SC', 'SD', 'TN', 'TX', 'UM', 'UT', 'VA', 'VI', 'VT', 'WA', 'WI', 'WV', 'WY'));

	add constraint make_name_check check(make in('Audi', 'Acura', 'BMW', 'Bentley', 'Buick', 'Cadillac', 'Chevrolet', 'Chrysler', 'Dodge', 'Ferrari', 'Fiat', 'Ford', 'GM', 'GEM', 'GMC', 'Honda', 'Hummer', 'Hyundai', 'Infiniti', 'Isuzu', 'Jaguar', 'Jeep', 'Kia', 'Lamborghini', 'Land Rover', 'Lexus', 'Lincoln', 'Lotus', 'Mazda', 'Mercedes-Benz', 'Mercury', 'Mitsubishi', 'Nissan', 'Oldsmobile', 'Peugeot', 'Pontiac', 'Porsche', 'Regal', 'Saab', 'Saturn', 'Subaru', 'Suzuki', 'Tesla', 'Toyota', 'Volkswagen', 'Volvo'));

	add constraint vtype_check check(vtype in('car', 'truck', 'suv'));

ALTER TABLE car
	add constraint type_check check(type in('compact', 'mid-size', 'large', 'subcompact', 'sports', 'convertible', 'minivan'));

alter table rent
	add constraint fk_rent_vin foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin);
alter table rent
	add constraint fk_rent_cid foreign key (cid) references customers(cid);

alter table truck
	add constraint fk_truck_vin foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin);

alter table suv
	add constraint fk_suv_vin foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin);

alter table car
	add constraint fk_car_vin foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin);

alter table service
	add constraint fk_service_vin foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin);

alter table reservation
	add constraint fk_reservation_vin foreign key (vin) references vehicle(vin);
alter table reservation
	add constraint fk_reservation_cid foreign key (cid) references customers(cid);
